<title>Document</title></head><body><div id="i58dde7eb2e524ad59314b608b8869f75_1"></div><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Georgia',serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">FactSet Reports Solid Results for First Quarter 2021</font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Georgia',serif;font-size:14pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Revenue increases 6% and EPS rises 8% </font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Georgia',serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">NORWALK, Conn., December&#160;21, 2020 - FactSet (&#34;FactSet&#34; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NYSE&#58;FDS) (NASDAQ&#58;FDS), a global provider of integrated financial information, analytical applications, and industry-leading service, today announced results for its first quarter ended November&#160;30, 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">First Quarter Fiscal 2021 Highlights</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Revenue increased 5.9%, or $21.5 million, to $388.2 million compared with $366.7 million for the same period in fiscal 2020. The increase is primarily due to higher sales of analytics and content and technology solutions (CTS).</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> Organic revenues grew 5.1%</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> to $386.7 million during the first quarter of fiscal 2021 from the prior year period. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) plus professional services was $1.56 billion at November&#160;30, 2020, compared with $1.48 billion at November&#160;30, 2019. The organic growth rate, which excludes the effects of acquisitions, dispositions, and foreign currency movements, was 5.0%. The primary contributors to this growth rate were higher sales in FactSet's research workflow solutions offset by lower sales in wealth and analytics. Please see the &#8220;ASV + Professional Services&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Operating margin increased to 31.2% compared with 30.9% for the same period last year. Adjusted operating margin improved to </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">34.3% compared with 33.9% in the prior year period primarily as a result of reduced employee-related operating expenses due to the coronavirus pandemic.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share (EPS) increased 7.8% to $2.62 compared with $2.43 for the same period in fiscal 2020. Adjusted diluted EPS rose 11.6% to $2.88 compared with $2.58 in the prior year period primarily driven by an improvement in operating results. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the first quarter increased to 15.8% compared with 13.6% a year ago, primarily due to an income tax benefit from a change in the foreign tax rate in the prior year as well as benefits related to finalizing the Company's tax returns with no similar event for the three months ended November 30, 2020.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet acquired Truvalue Labs, Inc., a pioneer in AI-driven environmental, social, and governance (ESG) data, in November 2020.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet reaffirms its annual outlook for fiscal 2021. Please see the &#8220;Annual Business Outlook&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">As previously disclosed on June 25, 2020, Scott Billeadeau retired from the Company's board of directors effective December 17, 2020. Lee Shavel has been appointed the new chair of FactSet's audit committee. </font></div><div style="padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;We have more conviction in our end markets than we did when we started the fiscal year,&#8221; said Phil Snow, FactSet CEO.  &#8220;Our pipeline remains robust, built on the investments we are making in content and technology.  The number and depth of conversations we are having with our largest clients around digital transformation, and how we can help streamline their workflows, position us well as we enter our second quarter.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;We continue to execute our plan diligently, with increased productivity and lower discretionary spend helping to fund our investment plans,&#8221; said Helen Shan, FactSet CFO. &#8220;We remain confident in our ability to deliver on both our annual targets and sustainable shareholder value, even through this period of pandemic uncertainty.&#8221; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) + Professional Services and Segment Revenue</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next twelve months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients. Professional services are revenues derived from project-based consulting and implementation.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV plus professional services was $1,562 million at November&#160;30, 2020. Organic ASV plus professional services was $1,557 million at November&#160;30, 2020, up $74.2 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 5.0%. Organic ASV, which excludes the effects of acquisitions, dispositions, and foreign currency movements, plus professional services, decreased $7.0 million over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates for the first quarter of fiscal 2020 were 5.1% and 4.4%, respectively. Buy-side clients accounted for approximately 84%</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> of organic ASV while the remainder was derived from sell-side firms that perform mergers and acquisitions advisory work, capital markets services, and equity research. Supplementary tables covering organic buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates may be found on the last page of this press release. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Americas region was $958.5 million, increasing 5.6% over the prior year period's $907.5 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Americas revenues for the quarter increased to $244.3 million compared with $231.3 million in the first quarter last year. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months, the Americas revenue growth rate was 5.6%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the EMEA region was $422.0 million, increasing 4.7% over the prior year period's $402.4 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">EMEA revenues were $105.8 million compared with $100.8 million from the first quarter of fiscal 2020. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the EMEA region revenue growth rate was 4.9%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Asia Pacific region was $156.5 million, increasing 9.5% over the prior year period's $143.9 million. Asia Pacific revenues were $38.1 million compared with $34.5 million from the first quarter of fiscal 2020. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Excluding the effects of acquisitions </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">2</font></div><div style="padding-right:18pt"><font style="color:#dcdcdc;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:6pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the Asia Pacific revenue growth rate was 10.4%. Segment ASV does not include professional services, which totaled $25.4 million at November&#160;30, 2020.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Operational Highlights &#8211; First Quarter Fiscal 2021</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Client count as of November&#160;30, 2020 was 5,939, a net increase of 64 clients in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in corporate and wealth management clients. The count includes clients with ASV of $10,000 and above.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">User count increased by 5,187 to 138,238 in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in wealth advisory users.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Annual ASV retention was greater than 95%. When expressed as a percentage of clients, annual retention was 90%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Employee count was 10,622 as of November&#160;30, 2020, up 7.7% over the last twelve months. Excluding the Truvalue Labs acquisition, headcount grew by 7.3% primarily driven by increased hiring in the Company's sales and content organizations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Net cash provided by operating activities decreased to $89.3 million compared with $95.8 million for the first quarter of 2020. Quarterly free cash flow increased to $70.9 million compared with $69.0 million a year ago, an increase of 2.8%, primarily due to lower capital expenditures.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Capital expenditures decreased to $18.3 million, compared with $26.8 million a year ago, primarily due to reduced facilities spend. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">A regular quarterly dividend of $29.1 million, or $0.77 per share, was paid on December&#160;17, 2020, to holders of record of FactSet&#8217;s common stock at the close of business on November&#160;30, 2020. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#4b4b4b;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet acquired Truvalue Labs, a San Francisco based company that applies AI-driven technology to over 100,000 unstructured text sources in 13 languages, including news, trade journals, and nongovernmental organizations and industry reports, to provide daily signals that identify positive and negative ESG behavior.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">The Company launched content and analytics for Danish covered bonds across its distribution channels, including the FactSet workstation. FactSet is working with Scanrate, a leading provider of fixed income software, models, and data for the Danish bond market, to deliver increased coverage of the Danish market.</font></div><div style="margin-top:12pt;text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:12pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Share Repurchase Program</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">FactSet repurchased 131,800 shares of its common stock for $43.1 million at an average price of $327.35 during the first quarter under the Company&#8217;s existing share repurchase program. style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">(a)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:8.24pt">GAAP operating income in the first quarter of fiscal 2021 was adjusted to exclude $6.2 million of pre-tax net expenses primarily related to professional fees and software development costs associated with the ongoing multi-year investment plan and severance, which reduced net income by $5.2 million and diluted earnings per share by $0.14. GAAP operating income in the first quarter of fiscal 2020 was adjusted to exclude $5.2 million of pre-tax net expenses primarily related to severance, stock-based compensation acceleration, professional fees related to infrastructure upgrade activities, and facilities costs, which reduced net income by $4.0 million and diluted earnings per share by $0.10. The income tax effect related to the other non-recurring items was $1.0 million in the first quarter of fiscal 2021 compared with $1.2 million for the same period in fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;padding-right:4.5pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">(b)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:8.24pt">Adjusted operating margin is calculated as adjusted operating income divided by GAAP revenues plus the deferred revenue fair value adjustment.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;padding-right:4.5pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">(c)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:8.68pt">For purposes of calculating adjusted net income and adjusted diluted earnings per share, intangible asset amortization, deferred revenue fair value adjustments and other non-recurring items were taxed at the annual effective tax rates of 15.8% for fiscal 2021 and 19.0% for fiscal 2020. </font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">(d)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:8.24pt">GAAP net income in the first quarter of fiscal 2020 was adjusted to exclude $3.5 million or $0.09 per share of income tax benefits primarily related to reserve adjustments and a change in tax rate of a foreign jurisdiction.
